with live data, such as fill/stroke colors, size, position, rotation, etc. Smooth animations can be created.\r\nThe graphics can be interactive and are capable of starting actions in web apps using the Synoptic API.\r\nThe powerful Vega charts engine can be directly used in the graphics to create and customize almost any type of BI-like charts.\r\nThe SCADAvis.io service provides the runtime
